my thesis for us today is , instead of building walls to create security , we need to build bridges .	我今天對我們的論點是 , 與其建造牆來創造安全感 , 我們需要建造橋樑 。
this is a famous bridge in europe .	這是歐洲一座有名的橋
it's the bridge over the drina river , the subject of a novel by ivo andrić , and it talks about how , in that very troubled part of europe and the balkans , over time there's been enormous building of walls .	它是一座橋樑 , 由ivoandriic所寫的小說主題 , 它談到如何在歐洲和巴爾幹半島有著巨大的牆壁 。
more recently , in the last decade , we begin to see these communities start , hesitatingly , to come together .	最近 , 在過去的十年裡 , 我們開始看到這些社區開始 , 猶豫著 , 聚集在一起 。
i would argue , again , opensource security is about connecting the international , the interagency , the privatepublic , and lashing it together with strategic communication , largely in social networks .	我會再次主張開放原始碼的安全性 , 重點在於連結國際、跨界、私人公開 , 並將之與戰略通訊 , 大致在社交網絡中 。
so let me talk a little bit about why we need to do that , because our global commons is under attack in a variety of ways , and none of the sources of threat to the global commons will be solved by building walls .	所以 , 讓我來談談為什麼我們需要這麼做 , 因為我們的全球公有物在各種方面受到攻擊 , 且對全球公有物的威脅 , 都不會被建造牆來解決 。
now , i'm a sailor , obviously .	現在 , 我是個水手 , 很顯然 ,
this is a ship , a liner , clipping through the indian ocean .	這是一艘船 , 一條線 , 穿過印度洋 。
what's wrong with this picture ?	這張照片有什麼問題 ?
it's got concertina wire along the sides of it .	沿著它的側邊有音樂電線 。
that's to prevent pirates from attacking it .	也就是防止海盜攻擊
piracy is a very active threat today around the world . this is in the indian ocean .	盜版是現今全世界非常活躍的威脅 。 這是在印度洋 。
piracy is also very active in the strait of malacca .	盜版在馬拉加的草根上也非常活躍 。
it's active in the gulf of guinea .	在幾內亞灣活躍起來
we see it in the caribbean .	我們在加勒比海看到的
it's a $10billionayear discontinuity in the global transport system .	在全球交通運輸系統中 , 是10億美元的不連續性 。
last year , at this time , there were 20 vessels , 500 mariners held hostage .	去年 , 在這個時候 , 有20艘船 , 500名馬林納人帶著人質 。
this is an attack on the global commons .	這是對全球公有物的攻擊 。
we need to think about how to address it .	我們需要思考如何處理它 。
let's shift to a different kind of sea , the cyber sea .	讓我們轉移到另一種海域 , 網路海域
here are photographs of two young men .	這裡有兩位年輕男性的照片 。
at the moment , they're incarcerated .	在當下 , 他們被監禁了 。
they conducted a credit card fraud that netted them over 10 billion dollars .	他們進行信用卡詐欺 , 將他們淨化超過一百億美元 。
this is part of cybercrime which is a $2trillionayear discontinuity in the global economy .	這是網路犯罪的一部分 , 是全球經濟體中2兆美元的不連續性 。
two trillion a year .	每年兩兆 。
that's just under the gdp of great britain .	那只是在英國的國內生產毛額下
so this cyber sea , which we know endlessly is the fundamental piece of radical openness , is very much under threat as well .	所以 , 我們所知的網路海 , 無止境地 , 是激進開放的基礎 , 同時也受到威脅 。
another thing i worry about in the global commons is the threat posed by trafficking , by the movement of narcotics , opium , here coming out of afghanistan through europe over to the united states .	另一件我在全球公有物中擔憂的事 , 就是販賣的威脅 , 由毒品、鴉片品的運動 , 從阿富汗到美國 。
we worry about cocaine coming from the andean ridge north .	我們擔心古柯鹼從andeanridge北部來 。
we worry about the movement of illegal weapons and trafficking . above all , perhaps , we worry about human trafficking , and the awful cost of it .	我們擔心非法武器和販賣的運動 。 最重要的 , 也許 , 我們擔心人口販賣 , 以及它的糟糕成本 。
trafficking moves largely at sea but in other parts of the global commons .	人口販賣主要在海上移動 , 但在全球公有物的其他部分 。
this is a photograph , and i wish i could tell you that this is a very hightech piece of us navy gear that we're using to stop the trafficking .	這是一張照片 , 我希望我能告訴你們 , 這是我們海軍的一塊非常高科技的 , 我們用它來阻止人口販賣 。
the bad news is , this is a semisubmersible run by drug cartels .	壞消息是 , 這是一個由毒品卡特爾執行的半信件 。
it was built in the jungles of south america .	建在南美洲叢林裡 。
we caught it with that lowtech raft — — and it was carrying six tons of cocaine .	我們用那個低科技的木筏抓到它 , 它帶著六噸的古柯鹼 。
crew of four . sophisticated communications sweep .	總共有四個 。 精密的溝通人員掃了 。
this kind of trafficking , in narcotics , in humans , in weapons , god forbid , in weapons of mass destruction , is part of the threat to the global commons .	這種販賣方式 , 在毒品、在人類、在武器、上帝禁止 , 在大規模毀滅的武器中 , 是對全球公有物的威脅的一部分 。
and let's pull it together in afghanistan today .	讓我們一起在阿富汗一起拉吧 。
this is a field of poppies in afghanistan .	這是一個在阿富汗的情人的領域 。
eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上百分之八十到九十的嬉皮、鴉片和海洛因 , 從阿富汗出來 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	我們也看到那裡 , 當然恐怖主義
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是蓋達組織的出發點 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個非常強烈的暴亂嵌在那兒 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的擔憂 , 也是全球公有物的一部分 , 我們必須處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以在這裡 , 21世紀
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們的20世紀工具是行不通的 。
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我主張我們不會只靠槍枝來傳遞安全感 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不會只從一把槍的桶子中得到安全感 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們會需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們做的時候 , 我們必須做得很好 , 同時要有競爭力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放原始碼的安全性 , 是關於國際、跨界、私人公開的聯繫 , 由這種在網路上策略性溝通的想法拉扯在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這如何用正面的方式運作 。
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 。 這些是阿富汗士兵 。
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很怪 。 我以為我讀到這個人口統計 , 二十多歲的年輕男女 , 在阿富汗大多不識字 。 」
you would be correct .	你會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 , 85%無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為什麼 ? 因為塔利班時期的教育 , 這些男女都學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書呢 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們讀識字課程 , 由nato和私營機構合作 , 與發展機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們已經教過超過20萬阿富汗安全部隊在基本層面上閱讀和寫作 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能在阿富汗讀和寫時 , 你通常會把筆放在口袋裡 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們會拿那支筆帶著好驕傲 , 把它放在口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這將國際組織起來 , 這項任務有50個國家 , 跨國界 , 這些發展機構 , 私人公共事業 , 來承擔這種保障 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	我們也在教他們戰鬥技能 , 當然 , 但我會主張 , 開放資源保障意味著用更長久的保障方式來連結 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	所謂的舒適感
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘叫 " 慈悲 " 的姐妹船 ,
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船隻 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這個 , 安慰 , 經營整個加勒比海和南美海岸進行病人治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	一般來說 , 他們會做四十萬個病人治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它不被軍隊嚴格地歸類 , 而是由人道組織的組合:操作希望 , 專案微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織會發送志願者
interagency physicians come out .	跨界醫師出來
they're all part of this .	他們都是這方面的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子來說明這會帶來的影響 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他的母親一起走了兩天 , 來到舒適的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他符合時 , 在他極其神秘的眼中 , 他突然抬頭說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	把這個乘以四十萬個病人的療法 , 這個私人的合作 , 與安全部隊合作 , 你開始用非常不同的角度看待創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	在這裡你看到棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能不能從這張照片中挑出兩名美國軍人士兵 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這些年輕男孩的兩位年輕男孩 。 這是一系列的棒球診所的一部分 , 在那裡 , 我們探索了大聯盟棒球之間的合作 , 國家部 , 他們設立了外交部 , 軍隊棒球選手 , 他們有真正的技能 , 但他們參與了這個任務 , 他們把診所放在拉丁美洲和加勒比海和加勒比海 , 在全加勒比海 , 全美各地 , 在加拉加拉加拉加拉加拉 , 加拉加拉加拉加州 , 加拉加拉加拉加拉加拉加拉 , 這裡 , 全市 , 加拉瓜 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它向年輕男性和女性的榜樣呈現關於健身以及我所主張的人生 , 幫助我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這種合作關係的另一個面向就是在災難中解脫 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是美國空軍直升機在2004年海嘯後參與 , 殺死了25萬人 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在這些重大災難中 , 2004年的海嘯 , 25萬人死亡 , 2005年巴基斯坦的卡什米里地震 , 8萬5千人死亡 , 海地地震 , 最近約有30萬人死於地震 , 最糟糕的地震組合 , 造成日本和它的核產業 , 在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到了國際間的合作夥伴 , 和私人機構合作 , 和安全合作 , 來處理這種天然災難 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	所以 , 這些都是開源安全的想法的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們將它結合起來 , 漸漸地 , 藉由這樣做的事情 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看到這個想法: 「 啊 , 阿 , 承認 , 這些一定是溝通的海道 , 或這些可能是光電纜線 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 。 這是根據推特的世界圖 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 , 綠色是地理分配 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成的 。
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	它是一個完美的提升了那個偉大的人口調查 , 世界上六大國家以下的順序:中國、印度、facebook、美國、推特和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	為什麼我們要進到這些網子裡 ?
why do we want to be involved ?	為什麼我們要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前談過阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦發表了一場這樣的演講 。 我說 , 如同我對大家說的 , 我在臉書上 , 朋友我 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	收到觀眾的笑聲 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	有一篇文章是阿普在電線上播放的 。
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	世界上兩個地方被拿起來:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約委託人需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上 , 我有數百個臉書朋友請求 , 來自印尼人和芬蘭人 , 大多是說: 「 承諾 , 我們聽說你需要一個朋友 , 順便說一下 , 北約是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	是啊 , 我們笑了 , 但這就是我們如何移動訊息 , 移動那個訊息就是我們如何聯繫國際 , 跨國 , 私人公開 , 而這些社交網絡來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我按個音符 。
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這張照片是一位勇敢的英國士兵
he's in the scots guards .	他在史考斯警衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在helmand的手錶 , 在阿富汗南部 。
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放在這裡提醒我們 , 我不會希望任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要有能力、有競爭力的軍隊來創造真正的軍事效果 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	這就是我們是誰以及我們所做的事的核心 , 我們為了保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍視的事物 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 要知道 , 生命不是一個開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有軍隊在戰鬥中 , 不論是在野蠻戰鬥中 , 都不需要軍隊 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會主張生命是鼻子 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你必須把它撥進去 , 正如我所想的 , 我們如何在21世紀創造安全性 , 將會有時候 , 我們會在真正的戰爭和危機中應用硬勢力 , 但有許多事會發生 , 如同我們今天所說 , 我們的軍隊可以成為創造21世紀的安全 , 國際 , 跨界 , 私人通訊 , 與強權聯繫在一起 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我會說 , 我們今天稍早聽到維基百科 。 我經常用維基百科來查閱事實 , 正如你們所有人所欣賞的 , 維基百科並不是被12位出色的人鎖在房間寫文章中 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天 , 都是成千上萬的人輸入資訊 , 每天數百萬人都在戒斷那些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是個完美的圖像 , 對於基本的觀點來說 , 沒有人像我們一起思考的那樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個聯盟 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人和我們所有人一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的遠見聲明非常簡單:一個每個人可以自由共享所有知識的總和世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 透過結合國際、跨國、私人、策略性的溝通 , 在這個21世紀 , 我們就能創造所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	謝謝大家 。 謝謝 。
